\newlength{\mtw}
\newcommand{\scaletext}[1]{%
    \settowidth{\mtw}{#1} % Measure text width
    \ifdim\mtw>2cm
        \resizebox{2cm}{!}{#1} % Scale only if it's wider than 2cm
    \else
        #1 % Otherwise, keep original size
    \fi
}

\newcommand{\T}[3]{
\begin{minipage}{2cm}
\begin{tabular}{c}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth, page=#1]{tangles-extra.pdf}\\[-0.5em]
\scaletext{{\small\ensuremath{#2}}}\\[-0.5em]
{\small\ensuremath{#3}}
\end{tabular}
\end{minipage}
}
